# 경쟁자배제 원문 로그

**Gamemaster:** 지난 탐사에서 여러분은 드로우들이 버려진 도시를 돌아다니고 있음을 발견했습니다.
지하에서 홀로 금지된 마법을 연구하는 마법사와 접촉해 같이 오리진을 공격하려는 계획이었죠.
여러분이 올린 보고를 받은 조사대장은 생각에 잠기더니
곧 동원 가능한 모든 모험가를 불러모았습니다.

**럭키:** "또 보던 얼굴들… 이 아니잖아!?"

**Gamemaster:** 전초기지를 밝혀주는 횃불빛이 흔들립니다.
여러분은 그의 천막에 모입니다.

**럭키:** "오! 새로운 모험가들이라니."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Dexterity (Stealth) Check19 🎲 1d20 + 5 + 4 = 19

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"지하는 흙 냄새가 나서 좋아한다."

**조사대장:** "이번에는 윗선에 말해서 가능한 많은 모험가를 불러달라고 했으니까요."

**럭키:** "드디어 오리진도 성장이라는걸 하는구나. 이 럭키 상병은 정말 기쁘다!"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"벌써 졸려."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** (보일듯 말듯 숨어 있습니다 정신을 집중해야 겨우 보이는군요)

**조사대장:** "인사할 시간을 드리고 싶지만 사안이 급하여 본론으로 들어가죠."

**라비니아:** "히에에엑…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"다 죽이면 된다, 아닌가?"

**조사대장:** 탁자 위에 거칠게 그린 지도가 펼쳐져 있고, 그 위에 말이 몇개 올려져 있습니다.
조사대장은 지도 위 한 지점을 손가락으로 짚습니다.

**라비니아:** "그렇긴합니다요"
"어차피 전부 비열한 드로우들입니다요"
@상습혐오

**조사대장:** "그건 맞지만 일각을 다투는 문제입니다."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"청소할 시간이 없어."

**팔슈:** unik
"금지된 마법사의 수준과 이름에 대해서 아는 바가 있나요? 배경은?"

**조사대장:** "적어도 전투용 호문쿨루스를 만들어낼 정도의 인물. 그 외엔 아직 암호문 해독중입니다."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** "드로우라는 자들은 평민들에게 하는 행동이 안좋은가?"

**조사대장:** "앞으로 조금이면 해독이 끝날 것 같지만요."

**럭키:** "흠. 우리가 본 피조물들 말이지?"

**라비니아:** "드로우들은 그냥 비열한 종족차별자들입니다요"

**럭키:** "그런걸 만들어내는 녀석이 좋은 놈이라고 보긴 어렵겠는걸."

**조사대장:** 끄덕입니다.

**라비니아:** (대충 자기 민족만 우월하다고 믿는 그런 애들이다
(콧수염은 안달려있다…!

**럭키:** "그 마법사란 녀석은 반드시 체포해야겠지만 그럴려면 일단 위치를 확보해야겠지."

**팔슈:** unik
"드로우는 여성우월적인 사회를 지니고 있습니다. 그들은 다른 종족을 하찮게 여기며, 노예, 실험
체로 다루는 종족입니다."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"나는 의뢰 내용에 따른다. 좋은 놈이건 안 좋은 놈이건 내게 중요치 않다."

**조사대장:** "좋기는 커녕 마법사 협회에 소식이 들리면 이 구역을 싹 불태워 버리러 올 정도입니다!"

**럭키:** "그런데 그 마법사. 자기가 원하면 드로우들이랑 그냥 접촉할 수 있던거 아닌가? 왜 이런 수수께
끼 놀이를 하면서 자길 찾게 만드는거지?"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"……"
"크흠."

**라비니아:** "마법사는 그냥 순수하게 금지된 마법을 연구하고싶은것 아닐까싶습니다요"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"같잖은 자존심 같은 거야."

**라비니아:** "히에엑"

**조사대장:** "제 생각엔… 드로우가 일방적으로 원하는게 아닐까 싶기도요."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"위저드들은… 자신들의 노력의 성과를 그렇게 쉽게 받아가기를 원치 않거든."
"괴팍해."

**팔슈:** unik
"다만, 모든 드로우가 그런것은 아니죠. 사냥의 여신을 따라 땅에서 올라온 드로우들은 선한측면
을 지니고 있습니다."

**럭키:** "그렇다면 일단은 마법사쪽에서 접촉을 피하고 있다고 가정해야겠네."

**팔슈:** unik
"거미여신 롤쓰를 따르는 지하의 드로우들은 대개 우호적이지 않다고 알고계시면됩니다."

**조사대장:** "그래요! 말 잘하셨습니다. 지금도 망할 롤쓰의 드로우들이 문제죠."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** "그럼 결정했군. 빨리 처리하도록 하세나"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"너, 아는 게 많군."

**럭키:** "중요한걸 말 안했잖아. 조사대장님. 그래서 당신이 지도 위에 짚은 곳에."
"흠… 우리가 세운 전초기지 처럼 놈들의 전초기지 그런걸려나?"

**조사대장:** "저희는 당신들이 잡아서 보낸 포로를 여러 방법으로 조사한 결과, 이 자리에 놈들의 지휘소가
있습니다."

**라비니아:** "드리즈트라고 짱짱 유명한 착한 드로우가 있었는데"

**럭키:** "이해했다. 거길 박살내면 마법사를 찾는 경쟁에서 우위를 점하겠군."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** "이 자리에?"

**라비니아:** "반면 그 사람 말고 착한 드로우는 세상에 남지 않을만큼 나쁜놈들뿐입니다요"

**조사대장:** "그렇죠. 해독이 끝나기 전에 놈들이 우연히 마법사와 접촉할 수도 있으니까요."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"반대로 이쪽이 찾아낼 정보를 취득할지도 몰라."

**럭키:** "아. 그리고 새로운 모험가가 늘어난거 좋기는 한데." 이리의 어깨를 툭 밀면서 말합니다
"얘 누가 데려왔어? 엄청 음침한데?"
"죽인다. 선악은 상관없다. 뭐 이런 사회성 결여된 녀석을."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"?"
"싸우자는 건가?"

**조사대장:** @카이젤린의 말에 끄덕입니다. "가능하면 그쪽에서 수집한 정보를 가져와 주세요. 그게 힘들면
불태우고."

**럭키:** "싸우자는 거냐고? 그건 너 하기에 달렸지."

**라비니아:** "히에에엑"
"라비니아가 데려왔습니다요"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"확인했어."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"의뢰에 맞춘다. 그 뿐이지."

**라비니아:** "같은 드루이드라서"

**럭키:** "잘 들어라. 음침한 녀석아. 이 몸은 수비대의 럭키 상병님이시다. 그리고 난 말썽 피우는 모험가
를 좋아하지 않아."
"오리진이랑 발더스 게이트에선 내 눈이 늘 지켜보고 있다고 생각하고 지내라고."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** (석궁으로 정확히 두 사람을 스칩니다)"그만, 거기까지"'
Crossbow, Light
Proficiency with a Light Crossbow allows you to add your proficiency bonus to
the attack roll for any attack you make with it.
🎲 1d20 + 5 + 2 = 10
🎲 1d8 + 5 = 13

**럭키:** "얌전히 말야."

**라비니아:** "히에엑…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"말썽이라면 내가 아닌 다른 놈이 피우고 있는데."

**팔슈:** unik
"선과 악의 구분없이 조화를 이루는 드루이드가 그런 발언이라니. 아, 혹시 그림자 집단을 따르
고 계신가요?"
"그렇다면 틀린 발언은 아니군요."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"…그리고 말이 와전되었군."
"내 말은, 의뢰의 내용에 따른다는 말이었다."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"어느 쪽이든 바람이 잘 드는 날이 없구나."

**조사대장:** "적어도 이런 일에는 안성맞춤인 인재들 아닙니까?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"내 이름은 갈기갈기 찢는 이리. 붉은 송곳니 부족 부족장 발자국 없는 범의 두 번째 아들이다."
"상병이라고 했나? 그건 어떤 계급이지?"

**럭키:** "대충. 병사들 중에서는 윗선이지."

**팔슈:** unik
"팔슈, 신화와 구전을 조사하는 조사관입니다. 당신의 부족은 어떤 회합이시죠?"

**럭키:** "간부는 아니고. 뭐. 정예 병사라고 생각해."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"회합…? 어려운 말은 모른다. 인간."

**라비니아:** "히에엑"
"일단, 정상적인 회합은 아닌것같습니다요…"
"뭔가 이질적입니다요"

**팔슈:** unik
"음… 그렇다면 어떤것이 특기이시죠? 배움 수준에 맞게 질문을 바꿔드리겠습니다."

**럭키:** "송곳니 부족? 거기 부족장 아드님이셔? 너희 부족으로 치면 상급 전사쯤으로 치면 되겠네."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"정예 병사라면… 족장은 아니군."

**럭키:** "아무튼 말야. 너희들 잘 들어. 이런 일 때문에 모험가는 필요하지. 하지만 모험가 중에선 본질이
용역 깡패에 지나지 않는 녀석들이 한 가득이야."
"그러니 착한 일만 하고 살아."
"불법적인 일 건들지 말고."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"오지랖이 넓다. 인간 수컷."

**럭키:** "원래 수비대원이 오지랖 없으면 못해먹을 직업이라서."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** (혹시 두 사람이 싸우고 집중이 몰린 와중에 갈취할 만한거 찾아서 훔치기 가능한가요?)

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"안그래도 부족민은 명예를 따른다."

**라비니아:** (크아악 그러지 말아다오

**Gamemaster:** (그러면 의뢰주가 어떻게 볼지는…

**라비니아:** (여긴 아군뿐이다…!

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"그리고… 특기라고 했나?"
"부순다."
"이게 특기다."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** (귀족이니 앞에서 욕만 안받으면 되긴하죠)

**럭키:** "그건 설명 안해도 알 것 같은데… 거기 석궁쟁이는 활이 특기야?"

**팔슈:** unik
"그렇군요. 평범한 교육을 받지 못했군요. 전투에서 관찰하겠습니다."

**럭키:** "양초쟁이는 얼마 전에 한 번 본 적이 있으니 대충 알겠고."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"그런고로… 조심하지. 도마뱀."
"시위는 함부로 놓는 게 아니다."

**자이릭스 에테리온:** "석궁은 2번째 무기고 1번째 무기는 다른게 있지. 지금은 주로 석궁을 쓴다"
"간지나잖냐"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"한 번은 넘어가겠다."

**라비니아:** "어쩐지 도망치고싶어지는 기분입니다요"

**럭키:** "이 몸은 대충 기동 강습병이라고 생각하면 된다. 빨리 움직이고 적의 약점을 친다."

**라비니아:** "으윽… 라비니아의 배가 갑자기 아파서…"

**조사대장:** "어딜 가십니까."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"재모집할 여력은 없어."

**라비니아:** "…"
"히에에엑…"
@눈물을 글썽이며 도망치려다가 돌아옵니다

**조사대장:** "…모험가란 자들에게 큰 기대를 갖진 않습니다만, 이번 일은 도시의 안위와 연결된 중요한 일
입니다."
"좀 진지해질 순 없는겁니까?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"난 지금 한없이 진지하다."

**럭키:** "전 늘 진지함돠~ 보십쇼, 조사대장님. 이마에 진지 라고 써져있지 않습니까."

**조사대장:** "말이나 못하면…"

**럭키:** "그리고 원래 모험가란 놈들 군기는 시작부터 잡아놔야 함돠~"
"이번에도 저희 경비대장님에게 말씀 잘 부탁드림다. 충성!"

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"네가 피곤한 사람이라 입 다무는 거라고 생각해."

**럭키:** "자 그럼. 출발할 준비할까."

**조사대장:** "그렇군요. 이번 기회를 경험삼아 다음부턴 제대로 잡도록 하죠 럭키 상병."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"졸립잖아."

**조사대장:** "그럼 여러분 이 지도를 가져가세요. 안 들키고 갈 길을 표시해 뒀습니다. 약간의 문제가 있지
만…"
"모험가니 알아서 잘 해결하시리라 믿습니다."

**라비니아:** "투명화 주문을 익혔어야했을것같습니다요…"

**자이릭스 에테리온:** (1개밖에 없나요 각각 1개씩인가요)

**조사대장:** 총 1개임미다

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"잠입 작전인가? 은신은 자신이 없다마는."

**럭키:** 지도 챙기고
"아니. 박살 작전이지."

**카이젤린:** 밀메0
"…또 '본 사람이 다 죽으면 은밀이다' 같은 거야?"

**럭키:** "자. 그럼 시야 넓고 발 빠른 사람이 척후를 맡아보실까? 음…" 일행을 번갈아 쳐다보다가
"…나구나."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면
"너다."

**팔슈:** unik
"본인이 나섰으니 뒤로 물러나지요."

**라비니아:** "멋집니다요..!"

**Produce Flame:** A flickering flame appears in your hand and remains there for the duration. While
there, the flame emits no heat and ignites nothing, and it sheds Bright Light in a
20-foot radius and Dim Light for an additional 20 feet. The spell ends if you cast it
again.
Until the spell ends, you can take a Magic action to hurl fire at a creature or an
object within 60 feet of you. Make a ranged spell attack. On a hit, the target takes
1d8 Fire damage.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11
(3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Sneak Attack
You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is
within 5 feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition,
and you don’t have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.
Crossbow, Light
Proficiency with a Light Crossbow allows you to add your proficiency bonus to
the attack roll for any attack you make with it.
🎲 2d20kh + 5 + 2 = 15
🎲 1d8 + 5 = 13

**unik:** Dancing Lights
You create up to four torch-size lights within range, making them appear as
torches, lanterns, or glowing orbs that hover for the duration. Alternatively, you
combine the four lights into one glowing Medium form that is vaguely humanlike.
Whichever form you choose, each light sheds Dim Light in a 10-foot radius.
As a Bonus Action, you can move the lights up to 60 feet to a space within range.
A light must be within 20 feet of another light created by this spell, and a light
vanishes if it exceeds the spell’s range.

(minimum of +1) if your AC is lower than that.

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).
Wrath of the Sea: Ongoing
🎲 5d6 = 21

**건강 내성 굴림20 🎲 1d20 + 2 + 3 =:** HP 업데이트 됨 두 배 적용 취소

**x:** 71-0(21)=71

**라비니아:** Depth Charge
With a boom that can be heard 300 feet away (or 1,000 feet in a liquid), a pulse
of thunder ripples out from a point you choose within range. Each creature in a
20-foot-radius sphere centred on that point must make a Constitution saving
throw. A target takes 7d6 thunder damage on a failed save, or half as much
damage on a successful one. This damage increases to 9d6 if the affected
creature is submerged in a liquid.
At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 3rd.
🎲 7d6 = 15

**라비니아:** Startling Speed
Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If
you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Sneak Attack
You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is
within 5 feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition,
and you don’t have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.
Crossbow, Light
Proficiency with a Light Crossbow allows you to add your proficiency bonus to
the attack roll for any attack you make with it.

**밀메:** Moonbeam
A silvery beam of pale light shines down in a 5-foot-radius, 40-foot-high Cylinder
centered on a point within range. Until the spell ends, Dim Light fills the
Cylinder, and you can take a Magic action on later turns to move the Cylinder
up to 60 feet.
When the Cylinder appears, each creature in it makes a Constitution saving
throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 2d10 Radiant damage, and if the
creature is shape-shifted (as a result of the Polymorph spell, for example), it
reverts to its true form and can’t shape-shift until it leaves the Cylinder. On a
successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only. A creature also
makes this save when the spell’s area moves into its space and when it enters
the spell’s area or ends its turn there. A creature makes this save only once per
turn.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d10 for each spell
slot level above 2.
🎲 2d10 = 5

**Fade Away:** You have learned to avoid notice at all costs, letting you momentarily obscure
yourself from observation. As a Bonus Action, you can take the Hide action to
conceal yourself without needing to be Heavily Obscured or behind Three-
Quarters Cover or Total Cover. You need not be out of a creature’s line of sight
to use this ability.
You become visible at the start of your next turn unless you have moved into a
position that allows you to use the Hide action normally. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, regaining all
expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

**🎲 1d20 + 3 + 2 =:** 럭키 gains 10 temp HP

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.
🎲 1d10 + 5 + 4 = 11

**Sneak Attack:** You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is within 5
feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition, and you don’t
have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

**드로우 견습 마술사:** 분쇄
사거리 내에서 당신이 지정한 지점에 엄청난 굉음이 터지며 울려퍼집니다. 해당 지점 반경
10ft 이내의 모든 크리처는 건강 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 3d8점의 천둥 피해를
입게 됩니다. 내성에 성공한 경우 피해는 절반으로 줄어듭니다. 만약 바위나 수정, 혹은 금속
등으로 만들어진 크리처가 주문에 영향을 받았을 경우, 해당 크리처는 내성 굴림에 불리함을
받게 됩니다.
주문의 범위 내에 다른 누군가가 장비하거나 들고 있지 않은 비마법적 물체가 있다면, 해당
물체 역시 피해를 받게 됩니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 피해가 1d8점씩 증가합니다.
🎲 3d8 = 18

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Sneak Attack
You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is
within 5 feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition,
and you don’t have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

**Dart:** Proficiency with a Dart allows you to add your proficiency bonus to the attack
roll for any attack you make with it.

**Dissolution:** You touch a creature or nonmagical object and break the target’s substance
down into its most fundamental components. Make a melee spell attack. On a
hit, the target takes 1d8 Force damage, and its AC is reduced by 1 against the
next attack roll made against it before the end of your next turn.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8),
11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).
🎲 1d20r1=1 + 4 + 2 = 9

**Fade Away:** You have learned to avoid notice at all costs, letting you momentarily obscure
yourself from observation. As a Bonus Action, you can take the Hide action to
conceal yourself without needing to be Heavily Obscured or behind Three-
Quarters Cover or Total Cover. You need not be out of a creature’s line of sight
to use this ability.
You become visible at the start of your next turn unless you have moved into a
position that allows you to use the Hide action normally. You can use this
feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, regaining all
expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**Sneak Attack:** You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is within 5
feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition, and you don’t
have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

Catastrophic Power: Ruinous Smite
You have mastered talents, both magical and martial, in your pursuit of the
inevitable destruction of mortals and their works. When you finish a Short or
Long Rest, you gain one of the following benefits until you finish your next Short
or Long Rest.
Elemental Cataclysm. As a Magic action, you can expend a spell slot to cause
elemental energy to burst in a 10-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within
60 feet of yourself. Choose a damage type: Acid, Cold, Fire, or Lightning.
Each creature in the Sphere must make a Dexterity saving throw against your
spell save DC. On a failed save, a creature takes 1d6 damage of the chosen type
per level of the spell slot expended, and then has Vulnerability to that damage
type for 1 minute. On a successful save, a creature takes half as much damage
only. The target repeats the save at the end of each of its turns, ending the
Vulnerability on a success.
Ruinous Smite. Once per turn when you deal damage with an attack with a
weapon or an Unarmed Strike, you can choose to expend a spell slot to deal an
extra 1d8 Necrotic damage, plus another 1d8 per level of the spell slot.
Weapon Mastery. Your supernatural connection to destruction allows you to
use the mastery property of one kind of weapon of your choice with which you
have proficiency, such as Shortbows or Quarterstaffs.
Whenever you finish a Long Rest, you can change the kind of weapon you
choose. For example, you could switch to using the mastery property of Slings
or Greatclubs.

니다. 다트는 모두 동시에 타격을 가하며, 하나의 목표에 다트를 모두 쏘거나 여러 목표에게

**카이젤린:** Moonbeam
A silvery beam of pale light shines down in a 5-foot-radius, 40-foot-high Cylinder
centered on a point within range. Until the spell ends, Dim Light fills the
Cylinder, and you can take a Magic action on later turns to move the Cylinder
up to 60 feet.
When the Cylinder appears, each creature in it makes a Constitution saving
throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 2d10 Radiant damage, and if the
creature is shape-shifted (as a result of the Polymorph spell, for example), it
reverts to its true form and can’t shape-shift until it leaves the Cylinder. On a
successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only. A creature also
makes this save when the spell’s area moves into its space and when it enters
the spell’s area or ends its turn there. A creature makes this save only once per
turn.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d10 for each spell
slot level above 2.

**Sneak Attack:** You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is within 5
feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition, and you don’t
have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

**Shifting:** As a Bonus Action, you can shape-shift to assume a more bestial appearance.
This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you revert to your normal
appearance as a Bonus Action. When you shift, you gain Temporary Hit Points
equal to 2 times your Proficiency Bonus. You can shift a number of times equal
to your Proficiency Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a
Long Rest.
Whenever you shift, you gain the benefit of one of the following options (choose
when you select this species)
Beasthide. You gain 1d6 additional Temporary Hit Points. While shifted, you
have a +1 bonus to your Armor Class.
Longtooth. When you shift and as a Bonus Action on your other turns while
shifted, you can use your elongated fangs to make an Unarmed Strike. If you hit
with this Unarmed Strike and deal damage, you can deal Piercing damage equal
to 1d6 plus your Strength modifier, instead of the normal damage of an
Unarmed Strike.
Swiftstride. While you are shifted, your Speed increases by 10 feet.
Additionally, you can move up to 10 feet as a Reaction when a creature ends its
turn within 5 feet of you. This reactive movement doesn’t provoke Opportunity
Attacks.
Wildhunt. While shifted, you have Advantage on Wisdom checks. Additionally,
no creature within 30 feet of you can have Advantage on an attack roll against
you unless you have the Incapacitated condition.
🎲 (2 * 2) + 1d6 = 8

**라비니아:** Item

**드로우 견습 마술사:** 분쇄
사거리 내에서 당신이 지정한 지점에 엄청난 굉음이 터지며 울려퍼집니다. 해당 지점 반경
10ft 이내의 모든 크리처는 건강 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 3d8점의 천둥 피해를
입게 됩니다. 내성에 성공한 경우 피해는 절반으로 줄어듭니다. 만약 바위나 수정, 혹은 금속
등으로 만들어진 크리처가 주문에 영향을 받았을 경우, 해당 크리처는 내성 굴림에 불리함을
받게 됩니다.
주문의 범위 내에 다른 누군가가 장비하거나 들고 있지 않은 비마법적 물체가 있다면, 해당
물체 역시 피해를 받게 됩니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 피해가 1d8점씩 증가합니다.

**라비니아:** Thunderwave
You unleash a wave of thunderous energy. Each creature in a 15-foot Cube
originating from you makes a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a
creature takes 2d8 Thunder damage and is pushed 10 feet away from you. On a
successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only.
In addition, unsecured objects that are entirely within the Cube are pushed 10
feet away from you, and a thunderous boom is audible within 300 feet.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for each spell
slot level above 1.
🎲 2d8 = 8

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Sneak Attack
You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is
within 5 feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition,
and you don’t have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

the attack roll for any attack you make with it.

**라비니아:** Thunderwave
You unleash a wave of thunderous energy. Each creature in a 15-foot Cube
originating from you makes a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a
creature takes 2d8 Thunder damage and is pushed 10 feet away from you. On a
successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only.
In addition, unsecured objects that are entirely within the Cube are pushed 10
feet away from you, and a thunderous boom is audible within 300 feet.
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for each spell
slot level above 1.
🎲 2d8 = 8

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Breath Weapon (Fire)
When you take the Attack action on your turn, you can replace one of your
attacks with an exhalation of magical energy in either a 15-foot Cone or a 30-
foot Line that is 5 feet wide (choose the shape each time). Each creature in that
area must make a Dexterity saving throw (DC 8 plus your Constitution modifier
and Proficiency Bonus). On a failed save, a creature takes 1d10 damage of the
type determined by your Draconic Ancestry trait. On a successful save, a
creature takes half as much damage. This damage increases by 1d10 when you
reach character levels 5 (2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).
You can use this Breath Weapon a number of times equal to your Proficiency
Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.
🎲 1d10 = 1

**드로우 마법사:** 화염구
당신의 손가락 끝에서 밝게 빛나는 섬광이 번쩍이며 사거리 내의 원하는 지점에 날아가 불꽃
을 일으키며 폭발합니다. 당신이 택한 지점에서 20ft 반경 내에 있는 모든 크리쳐는 민첩 내
성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 8d6점의 화염 피해를 받습니다. 내성에 성공할 경우 피해
는 절반으로 줄어듭니다.
이 주문의 효과는 모서리를 돌아 퍼져 나갑니다. 또한 이 주문은 해당 범위 내에서 누군가 장
비하거나 들고 있지 않은 가연성 물체에 모두 불을 붙입니다.
고레벨에서. 당신이 4레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 화염 피해가 1d6점씩 증가합니다.
🎲 8d6 = 31

**Identify:** You touch an object throughout the spell’s casting. If the object is a magic item
or some other magical object, you learn its properties and how to use them,
whether it requires Attunement, and how many charges it has, if any. You learn
whether any ongoing spells are affecting the item and what they are. If the item
was created by a spell, you learn that spell’s name.
If you instead touch a creature throughout the casting, you learn which ongoing
spells, if any, are currently affecting it.

**라비니아:** Shillelagh
A Club or Quarterstaff you are holding is imbued with nature’s power. For the
duration, you can use your spellcasting ability instead of Strength for the attack
and damage rolls of melee attacks using that weapon, and the weapon’s
damage die becomes a d8. If the attack deals damage, it can be Force damage
or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice).
The spell ends early if you cast it again or if you let go of the weapon.
Cantrip Upgrade. The damage die changes when you reach levels 5 (d10), 11
(d12), and 17 (2d6).

**Shifting:** As a Bonus Action, you can shape-shift to assume a more bestial appearance.
This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you revert to your normal
appearance as a Bonus Action. When you shift, you gain Temporary Hit Points
equal to 2 times your Proficiency Bonus. You can shift a number of times equal
to your Proficiency Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a
Long Rest.
Whenever you shift, you gain the benefit of one of the following options (choose
when you select this species)
Beasthide. You gain 1d6 additional Temporary Hit Points. While shifted, you
have a +1 bonus to your Armor Class.
Longtooth. When you shift and as a Bonus Action on your other turns while
shifted, you can use your elongated fangs to make an Unarmed Strike. If you hit
with this Unarmed Strike and deal damage, you can deal Piercing damage equal
to 1d6 plus your Strength modifier, instead of the normal damage of an
Unarmed Strike.
Swiftstride. While you are shifted, your Speed increases by 10 feet.
Additionally, you can move up to 10 feet as a Reaction when a creature ends its
turn within 5 feet of you. This reactive movement doesn’t provoke Opportunity
Attacks.
Wildhunt. While shifted, you have Advantage on Wisdom checks. Additionally,
no creature within 30 feet of you can have Advantage on an attack roll against
you unless you have the Incapacitated condition.
🎲 (2 * 2) + 1d6 = 6

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**🎲 1d10 + 5 + 4 =:** 럭키 takes 8 damage

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

**드로우 전사:** 민첩 내성 굴림19 🎲 1d20 + 4 + 3 + 0 = 19

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** 라면

**엄버 헐크:** Confusing Gaze
실패: 대상은 엄버 헐크의 다음 턴 시작까지 반응 행동을 할 수 없으며,다음 턴에 무엇을 할지
결정하기 위해 1d8을 굴립니다.
1~4. 대상은 아무 행동도 하지 않는다.
5~6. 대상은 행동이나 보너스 행동을 취하지 않고, 모든 이동력을 사용하여 무작위 방향으로
이동한다.
7~8. 대상은 사정거리 내의 무작위 생명체에게 근접 공격을 하거나, 공격할 수 없는 경우 아
무 행동도 하지 않는다.

**그리고 괴상한 정신파를 내뿜는군요:** Multiattack

**라비니아:** Wrath of the Sea
As a Bonus Action, you can expend a use of your Wild Shape to manifest a 5-
foot Emanation that takes the form of ocean spray that surrounds you for 10
minutes. It ends early if you dismiss it (no action required), manifest it again, or
have the Incapacitated condition.
When you manifest the Emanation and as a Bonus Action on your subsequent
turns, you can choose another creature you can see in the Emanation. The
target must succeed on a Constitution saving throw against your spell save DC
or take Cold damage and, if the creature is Large or smaller, be pushed up to 15
feet away from you. To determine this damage, roll a number of d6s equal to
your Wisdom modifier (minimum of one die).

**라비니아:** Startling Speed
Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If
you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.
기공 ㄱ
Shield (Enspelled Breastplate(쉴드))
An imperceptible barrier of magical force protects you. Until the start of your
next turn, you have a +5 bonus to AC, including against the triggering attack,
and you take no damage from Magic Missile.

**라비니아:** Spike Growth
The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Breath Weapon (Fire)
When you take the Attack action on your turn, you can replace one of your
attacks with an exhalation of magical energy in either a 15-foot Cone or a 30-
foot Line that is 5 feet wide (choose the shape each time). Each creature in that
area must make a Dexterity saving throw (DC 8 plus your Constitution modifier
and Proficiency Bonus). On a failed save, a creature takes 1d10 damage of the
type determined by your Draconic Ancestry trait. On a successful save, a
creature takes half as much damage. This damage increases by 1d10 when you
reach character levels 5 (2d10), 11 (3d10), and 17 (4d10).
You can use this Breath Weapon a number of times equal to your Proficiency
Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest.

**Ball Bearings:** As a Utilize action, you can spill Ball Bearings from their pouch. They spread to
cover a level, 10-foot-square area within 10 feet of yourself. A creature that

saving throw or have the Prone condition. It takes 10 minutes to recover the

**드로우 견습 마술사:** 마법 화살
당신은 마법의 힘으로 빛나는 3개의 다트를 만들어 냅니다. 각각의 다트는 사거리 내의, 당신
이 볼 수 있는 지정된 목표에게 날아가 명중합니다. 각각의 다트는 1d4 +1 역장 피해를 가합
니다. 다트는 모두 동시에 타격을 가하며, 하나의 목표에 다트를 모두 쏘거나 여러 목표에게
나누어 쏠 수 있습니다.
상위시전. 당신이 2레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 슬롯
레벨 하나당 추가로 다트를 하나 더 생성하여 발사할 수 있습니다.

**🎲 1d4 + 1 =:** 럭키 takes 6 damage

**카이젤린:** 카이젤린의 턴

**Magnify Gravity:** The gravity in a 10-foot-radius sphere centered on a point you can see within
range increases for a moment. Each creature in the sphere on the turn when
you cast the spell must make a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a
creature takes 2d8 force damage, and its speed is halved until the end of its
next turn. On a successful save, a creature takes half as much damage and
suffers no reduction to its speed.
Until the start of your next turn, any object that isn’t being worn or carried in
the sphere requires a successful Strength check against your spell save DC to
pick up or move.
At Higher Levels.When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or
higher, the damage increases by 1d8 for each slot level above 1st.
🎲 2d8 = 11

**Candle Pop:** 보너스 액션으로 심지 포인트 2점을 소모하여 모양이 일그러진 노란색 양초에 불을 붙이고 60
피트 이내에 있는 시야 내 생명체에게 던질 수 있습니다. 대상은 당신의 교활한 공격 난이도
(DC)에 대한 민첩성 내성 굴림에 성공해야 하며, 실패하면 양초의 일부가 왁스에 덮여 구속 상
태가 됩니다. 구속된 대상은 매 턴 종료 시 내성 굴림을 다시 시도하며, 성공하면 구속 효과가
해제됩니다.

**엄버 헐크:** 민첩 내성 굴림15 🎲 1d20 + 1 + 0 = 15

**Flooding Abundance:** 마법 행동으로, 심지 포인트 2점을 소모하여 티라이트 양초에 불을 붙이고 자신으로부터 60피
트 이내의 시야에 보이는 빈 공간에 던질 수 있습니다. 양초가 착지하면 1분 동안 15피트 정사
각형의 가연성 영역이 생성되며, 해당 영역은 지속 시간 동안 험지(Difficult Terrain)로 간주됩
니다. 불에 노출된 5피트 정사각형의 왁스는 3라운드에 걸쳐 완전히 타버리며, 그 안에 있는 생
명체는 턴을 시작할 때 2d6 화염 피해를 입습니다.

**럭키:** Deflect Attacks
When an attack roll hits you and its damage includes Bludgeoning, Piercing, or
Slashing damage, you can take a Reaction to reduce the attack’s total damage
against you. The reduction equals 1d10 plus your Dexterity modifier and Monk
level.
If you reduce the damage to 0, you can expend 1 Focus Point to redirect some
of the attack’s force. If you do so, choose a creature you can see within 5 feet of
yourself if the attack was a melee attack or a creature you can see within 60 feet
of yourself that isn’t behind Total Cover if the attack was a ranged attack. That
creature must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or take damage equal to two
rolls of your Martial Arts die plus your Dexterity modifier. The damage is the
same type dealt by the attack.

**🎲 1d10 + 5 + 4 =:** 럭키 takes 9 damage

Accelerate/Decelerate
This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the
instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force.
Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra
damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.
Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**🎲 4d6 =:** 드로우 전사 takes 14 damage

**럭키:** Open Hand Technique
Whenever you hit a creature with an attack granted by your Flurry of Blows, you
can impose one of the following effects on that target.
Addle. The target can’t make Opportunity Attacks until the start of its next turn.
Push. The target must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be pushed up to
15 feet away from you.
Topple. The target must succeed on a Dexterity saving throw or have the Prone
condition.

The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.
🎲 2d4 = 4

**자이릭스 에테리온:** Sneak Attack
You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is
within 5 feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition,
and you don’t have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

**드로우 견습 마술사:** 분쇄
사거리 내에서 당신이 지정한 지점에 엄청난 굉음이 터지며 울려퍼집니다. 해당 지점 반경
10ft 이내의 모든 크리처는 건강 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 3d8점의 천둥 피해를
입게 됩니다. 내성에 성공한 경우 피해는 절반으로 줄어듭니다. 만약 바위나 수정, 혹은 금속
등으로 만들어진 크리처가 주문에 영향을 받았을 경우, 해당 크리처는 내성 굴림에 불리함을
받게 됩니다.
주문의 범위 내에 다른 누군가가 장비하거나 들고 있지 않은 비마법적 물체가 있다면, 해당
물체 역시 피해를 받게 됩니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 피해가 1d8점씩 증가합니다.
🎲 3d8 = 13

The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

사거리 내에서 당신이 지정한 지점에 엄청난 굉음이 터지며 울려퍼집니다. 해당 지점 반경
10ft 이내의 모든 크리처는 건강 내성 굴림을 굴려야 하며, 실패할 시 3d8점의 천둥 피해를
입게 됩니다. 내성에 성공한 경우 피해는 절반으로 줄어듭니다. 만약 바위나 수정, 혹은 금속
등으로 만들어진 크리처가 주문에 영향을 받았을 경우, 해당 크리처는 내성 굴림에 불리함을
받게 됩니다.
주문의 범위 내에 다른 누군가가 장비하거나 들고 있지 않은 비마법적 물체가 있다면, 해당
물체 역시 피해를 받게 됩니다.
상위시전. 당신이 3레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 주문
슬롯 1레벨당 피해가 1d8점씩 증가합니다.

**Prestidigitation:** You create a magical effect within range. Choose the effect from the options
below. If you cast this spell multiple times, you can have up to three of its non-
instantaneous effects active at a time.
Sensory Effect. You create an instantaneous, harmless sensory effect, such as a
shower of sparks, a puff of wind, faint musical notes, or an odd odor.
Fire Play. You instantaneously light or snuff out a candle, a torch, or a small
campfire.
Clean or Soil. You instantaneously clean or soil an object no larger than 1 cubic
foot.
Minor Sensation. You chill, warm, or flavor up to 1 cubic foot of nonliving
material for 1 hour.
Magic Mark. You make a color, a small mark, or a symbol appear on an object
or a surface for 1 hour.
Minor Creation. You create a nonmagical trinket or an illusory image that can
fit in your hand. It lasts until the end of your next turn. A trinket can deal no
damage and has no monetary worth.

**Spike Growth:** The ground in a 20-foot-radius Sphere centered on a point within range sprouts
hard spikes and thorns. The area becomes Difficult Terrain for the duration.
When a creature moves into or within the area, it takes 2d4 Piercing damage for
every 5 feet it travels.
The transformation of the ground is camouflaged to look natural. Any creature
that can’t see the area when the spell is cast must take a Search action and
succeed on a Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check against your spell save DC
to recognize the terrain as hazardous before entering it.

**Gust of Wind:** A Line of strong wind 60 feet long and 10 feet wide blasts from you in a
direction you choose for the duration. Each creature in the Line must succeed
on a Strength saving throw or be pushed 15 feet away from you in a direction
following the Line. A creature that ends its turn in the Line must make the same
save.
Any creature in the Line must spend 2 feet of movement for every 1 foot it
moves when moving closer to you.
The gust disperses gas or vapor, and it extinguishes candles and similar
unprotected flames in the area. It causes protected flames, such as those of
lanterns, to dance wildly and has a 50 percent chance to extinguish them.
As a Bonus Action on your later turns, you can change the direction in which
the Line blasts from you.

**Startling Speed:** Your movements are so swift that you are almost invisible when in motion. If
you move at least 10 feet on your turn, attack rolls against you have
disadvantage until the start of your next turn. This feature does not function if
you are incapacitated or restrained. You can use this ability a number of rounds
per day equal to your level.

As a Utilize action, you can tie a knot with Rope if you succeed on a DC 10
Dexterity (Sleight of Hand) check. The Rope can be burst with a successful DC
20 Strength (Athletics) check.
You can bind an unwilling creature with the Rope only if the creature has the
Grappled, Incapacitated, or Restrained condition. If the creature’s legs are
bound, the creature has the Restrained condition until it escapes. Escaping the
Rope requires the creature to make a successful DC 15 Dexterity (Acrobatics)
check as an action.

**마법 화살:** 당신은 마법의 힘으로 빛나는 3개의 다트를 만들어 냅니다. 각각의 다트는 사거리 내의, 당신
이 볼 수 있는 지정된 목표에게 날아가 명중합니다. 각각의 다트는 1d4 +1 역장 피해를 가합
니다. 다트는 모두 동시에 타격을 가하며, 하나의 목표에 다트를 모두 쏘거나 여러 목표에게
나누어 쏠 수 있습니다.
상위시전. 당신이 2레벨 이상의 주문 슬롯을 사용하여 이 주문을 시전할 경우, 상승한 슬롯
레벨 하나당 추가로 다트를 하나 더 생성하여 발사할 수 있습니다.

Accelerate/Decelerate
This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the
instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force.
Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra
damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack.
Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0
damage).
Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage
increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**Sneak Attack:** You know how to strike subtly and exploit a foe’s distraction. Once per turn, you
can deal an extra 1d6 damage to one creature you hit with an attack roll if you
have Advantage on the roll and the attack uses a Finesse or a Ranged weapon.
The extra damage’s type is the same as the weapon’s type.
You don’t need Advantage on the attack roll if at least one of your allies is within 5
feet of the target, the ally doesn’t have the Incapacitated condition, and you don’t
have Disadvantage on the attack roll.
The extra damage increases as you gain Rogue levels, as shown in the Sneak
Attack column of the Rogue Features table.

**Prestidigitation:** You create a magical effect within range. Choose the effect from the options
below. If you cast this spell multiple times, you can have up to three of its non-
instantaneous effects active at a time.
Sensory Effect. You create an instantaneous, harmless sensory effect, such as a
shower of sparks, a puff of wind, faint musical notes, or an odd odor.
Fire Play. You instantaneously light or snuff out a candle, a torch, or a small
campfire.
Clean or Soil. You instantaneously clean or soil an object no larger than 1 cubic
foot.
Minor Sensation. You chill, warm, or flavor up to 1 cubic foot of nonliving
material for 1 hour.
Magic Mark. You make a color, a small mark, or a symbol appear on an object
or a surface for 1 hour.
Minor Creation. You create a nonmagical trinket or an illusory image that can
fit in your hand. It lasts until the end of your next turn. A trinket can deal no
damage and has no monetary worth.
